Kalimetrix Logiscope Quality Report    

Date: 16 Oct 2015

This document contains information concerning the quality analysis of the project PopcornTime Android made with Logiscope QualityChecker which is part of Kalimetrix Logiscope.

The following levels of information are available:

  • Application
  • Packages
  • Modules
  • Classes
  • Functions & Methods
  • Source files list

Application Level

The following levels are available for Application analysis:

  • Factor level
  • Criteria level
  • Metric level

  • The name of the factor.
  • The list of categories (the one which applies to the application is in red).

Application Factor Description

Factor : STATISTICS

This factor applies to Application for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the factor is :

STATISTICS = SIZE

 Application statistics: for statistical and information purposes only.

Packages Factor Description

Factor : MAINTAINABILITY

This factor applies to Packages for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the factor is :

MAINTAINABILITY = ANALYZABILITYp + CHANGEABILITYp + STABILITYp + TESTABILITYp

 MAINTAINABILITY: the capability of the software product to be modified. 
Modifications may include corrections, improvements or adaptation 
of the software to changes in environment, and in requirements 
and functional specifications [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Modules Factor Description

Factor : MAINTAINABILITY

This factor applies to Modules for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the factor is :

MAINTAINABILITY = ANALYZABILITYm + CHANGEABILITYm + STABILITYm + TESTABILITYm

 MAINTAINABILITY: the capability of the software product to be modified. 
Modifications may include corrections, improvements or adaptation 
of the software to changes in environment, and in requirements 
and functional specifications [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Classes Factor Description

Factor : MAINTAINABILITY

This factor applies to Classes for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the factor is :

MAINTAINABILITY = ANALYZABILITYc + CHANGEABILITYc + STABILITYc + TESTABILITYc

 MAINTAINABILITY: the capability of the software product to be modified. 
Modifications may include corrections, improvements or adaptation 
of the software to changes in environment, and in requirements 
and functional specifications [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Functions Factor Description

Factor : MAINTAINABILITY

This factor applies to Functions for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the factor is :

MAINTAINABILITY = ANALYZABILITY + CHANGEABILITY + STABILITY + TESTABILITY

 MAINTAINABILITY: the capability of the software product to be modified. 
Modifications may include corrections, improvements or adaptation 
of the software to changes in environment, and in requirements 
and functional specifications [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Application Criteria Description

Criteria : SIZE

This criteria applies to Application for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

SIZE = ap_stat + ap_func + ap_sline + ap_vg + ap_wmc + ap_eloc + ap_comf + ap_inhg_levl

   Application Size is based on :
  - Number of executable statements 
  - Number of functions
  - Total number of lines
  - Sum of cyclomatic numbers
  - Weighted methods per application
  - Number of effective lines of code
  - Comment rate
  - Depth of inheritance

Packages Criteria Description

Criteria : ANALYZABILITYp

This criteria applies to Packages for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

ANALYZABILITYp = pk_vg + pk_comf + pk_inh_levl_max + pk_pkused

  ANALYZABILITY: the capability of the sofware product 
 to be diagnosed for deficiencies or causes of failures
 in the software, or for the parts to be modified to be 
 identified [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Criteria : CHANGEABILITYp

This criteria applies to Packages for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

CHANGEABILITYp = pk_stmt + pk_file + pk_func + pk_data

  CHANGEABILITY: the capability of the software product
 to enable a specified modification to be implemented
 [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Criteria : STABILITYp

This criteria applies to Packages for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

STABILITYp = pk_data_publ + pk_func_publ + pk_class + pk_inh

  STABILITY: the capability of the software product to 
 avoid unexpected effects from modifications of the
 software [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Criteria : TESTABILITYp

This criteria applies to Packages for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

TESTABILITYp = pk_vg + pk_func + pk_inh + pk_class

  TESTABILITY: the capability of the software product to
 enable modified software to be validated [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Modules Criteria Description

Criteria : ANALYZABILITYm

This criteria applies to Modules for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

ANALYZABILITYm = md_comf + md_line + md_import_pack

  ANALYZABILITY: the capability of the sofware product 
 to be diagnosed for deficiencies or causes of failures
 in the software, or for the parts to be modified to be 
 identified [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Criteria : CHANGEABILITYm

This criteria applies to Modules for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

CHANGEABILITYm = md_stat + md_dclstat + md_class

  CHANGEABILITY: the capability of the software product
 to enable a specified modification to be implemented
 [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Criteria : STABILITYm

This criteria applies to Modules for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

STABILITYm = md_dclstat + md_class + md_interf

  STABILITY: the capability of the software product to 
 avoid unexpected effects from modifications of the
 software [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Criteria : TESTABILITYm

This criteria applies to Modules for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

TESTABILITYm = md_stat + md_class + md_import

  TESTABILITY: the capability of the software product to
 enable modified software to be validated [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Classes Criteria Description

Criteria : ANALYZABILITYc

This criteria applies to Classes for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

ANALYZABILITYc = cl_wmc + cl_comf + in_bases + cu_cdused

  ANALYZABILITY: the capability of the sofware product 
 to be diagnosed for deficiencies or causes of failures
 in the software, or for the parts to be modified to be 
 identified [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Criteria : CHANGEABILITYc

This criteria applies to Classes for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

CHANGEABILITYc = cl_stat + cl_func + cl_data

  CHANGEABILITY: the capability of the software product
 to enable a specified modification to be implemented
 [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Criteria : STABILITYc

This criteria applies to Classes for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

STABILITYc = cl_data_publ + cu_cdusers + in_noc + cl_func_publ

  STABILITY: the capability of the software product to 
 avoid unexpected effects from modifications of the
 software [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Criteria : TESTABILITYc

This criteria applies to Classes for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

TESTABILITYc = cl_wmc + cl_func + cu_cdused

  TESTABILITY: the capability of the software product to
 enable modified software to be validated [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Functions Criteria Description

Criteria : ANALYZABILITY

This criteria applies to Functions for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

ANALYZABILITY = ct_vg + avg_size + com_freq + lc_stat

  ANALYZABILITY: the capability of the sofware product 
 to be diagnosed for deficiencies or causes of failures
 in the software, or for the parts to be modified to be 
 indentified [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Criteria : CHANGEABILITY

This criteria applies to Functions for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

CHANGEABILITY = voc_freq + n2 + ct_nest

  CHANGEABILITY: the capability of the software product
 to enable a specified modification to be implemented
 [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Criteria : STABILITY

This criteria applies to Functions for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

STABILITY = struc_pg + ct_nest + ct_npath

  STABILITY: the capability of the software product to 
 avoid unexpected effects from modifications of the
 software [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Criteria : TESTABILITY

This criteria applies to Functions for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the criteria is :

TESTABILITY = ct_vg + ic_param + ct_npath

  TESTABILITY: the capability of the software product to
 enable modified software to be validated [ISO/IEC 9126-1:2001].

Application Metric Description

Metric : Average complexity of functions (ap_wmc)

This metric applies to Application for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the metric is :

ap_wmc = (ap_vg) / (ap_func)

 Average cyclomatic number (VG) of the functions defined in the project:
  ap_wmc = ap_vg / ap_func
  where:
	ap_vg is the sum of the cyclomatic numbers of the functions,
	ap_func is the number of functions in the application.

Metric : Application comment rate (ap_comf)

This metric applies to Application for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the metric is :

ap_comf = (ap_scomm) / (ap_sline)

 Percentage of comments in the project source files:
  ap_comf = ap_scomm / ap_sline
  where:
	ap_scomm is the number of lines of comments in the project source files,
	md_line is the total number of lines in the project source files.

Metric : Application effective lines of code (ap_eloc)

This metric applies to Application for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the metric is :

ap_eloc = ap_sloc - ap_ssbra

 Total number of effective lines of code in the project source files;
Empty lines, lines of comments or lines containing only lone braces 
are not counted:
  ap_eloc = ap_sloc - ap_ssbra
  where:
	ap_sloc is the number of lines of code in the project source files,
	ap_ssbra is the number of lines containing only lone braces 
                   in the project source files.

Metric : Number of statements (ap_stat)

This metric applies to Application for JAVA language.

 

Total number of statements in the application (sum of lc_stat for all functions or methods).

Metric : Number of application functions (ap_func)

This metric applies to Application for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as LMA.

 

This metric contains the total number of application functions.

Metric : Number of lines (ap_sline)

This metric applies to Application for JAVA language.

 
Number of physical lines in the application.

Metric : Sum of cyclomatic numbers of the application functions (ap_vg)

This metric applies to Application for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as ap_cyclo, VGA.

 

Sum of cyclomatic numbers (VG) for all functions in the application.

Metric : Depth of inheritance tree (ap_inhg_levl)

This metric applies to Application for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as GH_LEVL.

 

The depth of the inheritance tree is the number of classes in the longest inheritance link.

Metric : Number of lines of comments (ap_scomm)

This metric applies to Application for JAVA language.

 
Number of lines containing comments in the application.

Metric : Number of lines of code (ap_sloc)

This metric applies to Application for JAVA language.

 
Number of lines containing executable code in the application.

Metric : Number of lines with lone braces (ap_ssbra)

This metric applies to Application for JAVA language.

 
Number of lines containing only one brace { or } in the application
(only Begin / End  for Ada).

Packages Metric Description

Metric : Package comment rate (pk_comf)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the metric is :

pk_comf = (pk_com) / (pk_line MAX 1)

 Ratio between the number of lines of comments in the package 
and the total number of statements:
  pk_comf = pk_comm / pk_line
  where:
	pk_comm is the number of lines of comments in the package,
	pk_stmt is the total number of lines in the package.

Metric : Total number of inheritance (pk_inh)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the metric is :

pk_inh = pk_extend + pk_implement

 Number of inheritance using extend and/or implement in the package

Metric : Number of classes (pk_class)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Total number of classes declared in the package.

Metric : Number of attributes (pk_data)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Total number of attributes declared in the package.

Metric : Number of public attributes (pk_data_publ)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Total number of attributes declared with the keyword public in the package.

Metric : Number of functions (pk_func)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Total number of functions declared in the package.

Metric : Number of public functions (pk_func_publ)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Total number of functions declared with the keyword public in the package.

Metric : Total number of extends (pk_extend)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Number of classes referenced in the extend directives of the classes in
the packages.
If a class is referenced several times it is counted several times.

Metric : Total number of implement (pk_implement)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Number of classes referenced in the implement directives of the classes
in the packages.
If a class is referenced several times it is counted several times.

Metric : Number of interfaces (pk_interf)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Total number of interfaces declared in the package.

Metric : Number of files (pk_file)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Number of files containing descriptions of classes of the package.

Metric : Maximum level of inheritance for classes (pk_inh_levl_max)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Maximum length of an inheritance chain starting from a class declared in
the package.

Metric : Number of used packages (pk_pkused)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Total number of packages imported by classes of the package.

Metric : Number of statements (pk_stmt)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Total number of executable statements in functions of the package.

Metric : Sum of cyclomatic numbers (pk_vg)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Sum of Cyclomatic Numbers (ct_vg) of the functions declared in the
classes of the package.

Metric : Number of lines of comment (pk_com)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Total number of comment lines in a package.
Comments located outside the package are not counted.

Metric : Number of lines (pk_line)

This metric applies to Packages for JAVA language.

 

Total number of lines for the files containing the package.

Modules Metric Description

Metric : Module comment rate (md_comf)

This metric applies to Modules for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the metric is :

md_comf = (md_comm) / (md_line)

 Ratio between the number of lines of comments in the module 
and the number of lines:
  md_comf = md_comm / md_line
  where:
	md_comm is the number of lines of comments in the module,
	md_line is the total number of lines in the module.

Metric : Module declarations (md_import)

This metric applies to Modules for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the metric is :

md_import = md_import_demd + md_import_pack + md_import_type

 Number of data imported in the module:
  md_import = md_import_pack + md_import_type + md_import_demd 
  where:
	md_import_pack is the number of imported packages,
	md_import_type is the number of imported types,
	md_import_demd is the number of importation on demand.

Metric : Number of classes (md_class)

This metric applies to Modules for JAVA language.

 

Number of classes declared at the first level of a module.

Metric : Number of interfaces (md_interf)

This metric applies to Modules for JAVA language.

 

Number of interfaces declared at the first level of a module.

Metric : Number of lines (md_line)

This metric applies to Modules for JAVA language.

 
Number of physical lines in the module.

Metric : Number of statements (md_stat)

This metric applies to Modules for JAVA language.

 

Number of statements that can be executed in a module.
The following are statements:

	;(empty statement)		
	IF [ELSE]	SWITCH
	DO		FOR		WHILE		
	GOTO		BREAK		CONTINUE
	RETURN		THROW		TRY		ASM
	expression;(simple statement)
	function definition
	variable declaration

Statements located in the external declarations are not taken into account.

For a detailed specification of executable statements in the project programming language 
please refer to the corresponding Logiscope - QualityChecker and RuleChecker - Reference Manual.

Metric : Number of declarative statements (md_dclstat)

This metric applies to Modules for JAVA language.

 

Number of declaration in the method bodies of a module.

Metric : Number of imported packages (md_import_pack)

This metric applies to Modules for JAVA language.

 

Number of packages appearing in the import statements of a module.
The parameter of the import statement is supposed to be a package name
if it is a simple name (without a dot in it) or if it is not used as a
type in the module.

Metric : Number of lines of comments (md_comm)

This metric applies to Modules for JAVA language.

 
Number of lines containing comments in a module.

Metric : Number of importations on demand (md_import_demd)

This metric applies to Modules for JAVA language.

 

Number of import statements in a module whose parameter is a
generic name (ended by .*).

Metric : Number of imported types (md_import_type)

This metric applies to Modules for JAVA language.

 

Number of types appearing in the import statements of a module.
The parameter of the import statement is supposed to be a type name
if it is not a simple name (with at least a dot in it) or if it is
used as a type in the module.

Classes Metric Description

Metric : Class comment rate (cl_comf)

This metric applies to Classes for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the metric is :

cl_comf = (cl_comm) / (cl_line MAX 1)

 Ratio between the number of lines of comments in the module 
and the total number of lines:
  cl_comf = cl_comm / cl_line
  where:
	cl_comm is the number of lines of comments in the package,
	cl_line is the total number of lines in the package.

Metric : Total number of attributes (cl_data)

This metric applies to Classes for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as cl_field.

 

Total number of attributes declared inside the class declaration

Metric : Total number of methods (cl_func)

This metric applies to Classes for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as cl_meth.

 

Total number of methods declared inside the class declaration

Metric : Number of statements (cl_stat)

This metric applies to Classes for JAVA language.

 

Number of executable statements in all methods and initialization code of a class.

For a detailed specification of executable statements in the project programming language 
please refer to the corresponding Logiscope - QualityChecker and RuleChecker - Reference Manual.

Metric : Weighted Methods per Class (cl_wmc)

This metric applies to Classes for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as cl_cyclo, LMVG.

 

Sun of the static complexities of the class methods. 
Static complexity is represented by the cyclomatic number of the functions.
	cl_wmc = SUM (ct_vg)

Metric : Number of direct used classes (cu_cdused)

This metric applies to Classes for JAVA language.

 

Number of classes used directly by the current class.

Metric : Number of direct users classes (cu_cdusers)

This metric applies to Classes for JAVA language.

 

Number of classes which use directly the current class.

Metric : Number of base classes (in_bases)

This metric applies to Classes for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as in_inherits.

 

Number of classes from which the class inherits directly or not.
If multiple inheritance is not used the value of in_bases is equal to the value
of in_depth.

Metric : Number of children (in_noc)

This metric applies to Classes for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as in_dderived, NOC.

 

Number of classes which directly inherit from the current class.

Metric : Number of public methods (cl_func_publ)

This metric applies to Classes for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as cl_meth_publ, LMPU.

 

Number of methods declared in the public section.

Metric : Number of public attributes (cl_data_publ)

This metric applies to Classes for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as cl_field_publ, LAPU.

 

Number of attributes declared in the public section or in the public interface
of a Java class.

Metric : Number of lines of comment (cl_comm)

This metric applies to Classes for JAVA language.

 

Number of comment lines in a class.

Metric : Number of lines (cl_line)

This metric applies to Classes for JAVA language.

 

Total number of lines in a class or an interface.

Functions Metric Description

Metric : Average size of statements (avg_size)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the metric is :

avg_size = (N1 + N2) / (lc_stat MAX 1)

 Average number of operands and operators per executable statement:
	avg_size = N1+N2 / lc_stat;
	where:
	N1 is the number of operator occurrences,
	N2 is the number of operand occurrences,
	lc_stat is the number of statements in the function.

Metric : Vocabulary frequency (voc_freq)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the metric is :

voc_freq = (N1 + N2 MAX 1) / (n1 + n2 MAX 1)

 Average number of times the vocabulary is used:
	voc_freq = (N1+N2) / (n1+n2)
	where :
	N1 is the number of operator occurrences,
	N2 is the number of operand occurrences,
	n1 is the number of distinct operators,
	n2 is the number of distinct operands.

Metric : Comment frequency (com_freq)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the metric is :

com_freq = (lc_ccomm) / (lc_stat MAX 1)

 Ratio between the number of lines of comments in the function 
and the number of statements:
  com_freq = lc_ccomm / lc_stat
  where:
	lc_ccomm is the number of lines of comments in the function,
	lc_stat is the number of instructions in the function.

Metric : Structuring (struc_pg)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the metric is :

struc_pg = ct_bran + ct_exit MAX 1

 Number of violations of Structured Programming:
   - ct_bran : No break or continue in a loop,
   - ct_exit : No auxilary exit.

Metric : FunctionMetric_1 (FunctionMetric_1)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

The formula to compute the metric is :

FunctionMetric_1 = avg_size

Metric : Maximum nesting level (ct_nest)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

 

Maximum number of control structure nested levels in a function.

Metric : Number of non-cyclic paths (ct_npath)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

 

Number of non-cyclic execution paths.
It is calculated according to the transfers of control induced by the various
types of statement. The PATH for a sequence of statements with the same nesting
level is the product of each statement's PATH. For nested structures the
sum of the PATH is calculated.
Therefore:
	PATH (if then else endif) = PATH (body of then) + PATH (body of else)
	PATH (while do - endwhile) = PATH (body of while) + 1
	PATH (case of - endcase) = SUM(i=1n) PATH (body of ist case)
where n is the number of cases.
	PATH (sequence) = 1

Metric : Cyclomatic number (VG) (ct_vg)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as ct_cyclo, VG.

 

Cyclomatic number of the control graph of the function
In the graph theory the Cyclomatic number V(g) gives the number of linearly
independent paths in a connected graph. 
For a  connected graph g the cyclomatic
number is calculated as follows:
	V(g) = E - N + 1
	where:
	E is the number of edges between the graph's nodes
	N is the number of nodes in the graph.
For a control graph which is not a  connected graph since it has one or several
entries and one or several exits the cyclomatic number is given by the formula:
	V(g) = E - N + 2 + AEn + AEx
	where:
	E is the number of edges between a graph's nodes
	N is the number of nodes in the graph
	AEn is the number of auxiliary entries
	AEx is the number of auxiliary exits

This metric is often use as an indicator of the minimum number of test cases 
to be exercised on the function. 
For more details please refer to Logiscope QualityChecker - Basic Concepts manual.

Metric : Number of parameters (ic_param)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as PARA.

 

Number of formal parameters in the function.

Metric : Number of statements (lc_stat)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as STMT.

 

Number of executable statements in the function.
The following are usually considered as executable statements:

	;(empty statement)  
      IF [ELSE]	SWITCH
	DO		FOR		WHILE	
      GOTO		BREAK		CONTINUE
	RETURN	THROW		TRY		ASM
	expression;(simple statement)
	function definition 
	variable declaration 

Statements located in the external declarations are not taken into account.

For a detailed specification of executable statements in the project programming language 
please refer to the corresponding Logiscope - QualityChecker and RuleChecker - Reference Manual.

Metric : Number of distinct operands (n2)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as ha_dopd.

 

Number of different operands used in the function.

For a detailed specification of operands in the project programming language 
please refer to the corresponding Logiscope - QualityChecker and RuleChecker - Reference Manual.

Metric : Total number of operators (N1)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as ha_topt.

 

Total number of operators used in the function.

For a detailed specification of operators in the project programming language 
please refer to the corresponding Logiscope - QualityChecker and RuleChecker - Reference Manual.

Metric : Total number of operands (N2)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as ha_topd.

 

Total number of operands used in the function.

For a detailed specification of operands in the project programming language 
please refer to the corresponding Logiscope - QualityChecker and RuleChecker - Reference Manual.

Metric : Number of distinct operators (n1)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as ha_dopt.

 

Number of different operators used in the function.

For a detailed specification of operators in the project programming language 
please refer to the corresponding Logiscope - QualityChecker and RuleChecker - Reference Manual.

Metric : Number of lines of comments (lc_ccomm)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

 
Number of lines containing comments in a component.

Metric : Number of destructuring statements (ct_bran)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

 

Number of goto break (not included in a switch) or continue statements in the function.
For Structured Programming ct_bran shall be equal to 0
(i.e. each structure shall have a single exit point).

Metric : Number of out statements (ct_exit)

This metric applies to Functions for JAVA language.

For compatibility reasons this metric is also known as N_OUT.

 

Number of return or exit statements in the function.
For Structured Programming ct_exit shall be equal to 1
(i.e. the function shall have a single exit point).
